| 1:39:17| It had to be on.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=5957)|
| 1:39:20| So I'd like to talk about to lobby or advocate,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=5960)|
| 1:39:22| our board responsibilities, my responsibilities,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=5962)|
| 1:39:25| TSBA's role, and the call for resolutions.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=5965)|
| 1:39:30| While we often try to keep from using a disliked word,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=5970)|
| 1:39:33| in some cases it just isn't reasonable,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=5973)|
| 1:39:35| and lobbying is one of those words that sometimes people don't like.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=5975)|
| 1:39:39| But when words have definitions that are in statute,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=5979)|
| 1:39:42| we need to use the right one.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=5982)|
| 1:39:44| And in the case of lobbying or advocacy, word choice matters,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=5984)|
| 1:39:47| and it's important for factual transparency.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=5987)|
| 1:39:51| A lobbyist is any person who engages in lobbying for compensation.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=5991)|
| 1:39:56| Clearly I and we are not lobbyists.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=5996)|
| 1:40:00| Lobbying does not make one a lobbyist,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6000)|
| 1:40:03| but lobbying for compensation makes one a lobbyist.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6003)|
| 1:40:06| There are also other rules related to the amount of lobbying one does that| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6006)|
| 1:40:09| would require an individual to register as a volunteer lobbyist.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6009)|
| 1:40:13| However, this also does not apply to us as a board or as individuals.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6013)|
| 1:40:19| Lobbying is actually a responsibility of our office.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6019)|
| 1:40:24| So to lobby is to communicate directly or indirectly with any official in| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6024)|
| 1:40:29| the legislative branch or executive branch for the purpose of influencing| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6029)|
| 1:40:33| any legislative action or administrative action.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6033)|
| 1:40:37| So if we are talking to our legislators| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6037)|
| 1:40:40| and we are asking them to do something specific with a bill,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6040)|
| 1:40:44| if we are asking them to pass a bill,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6044)|
| 1:40:46| if we are asking them to move legislation forward,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6046)|
| 1:40:49| if we are asking them to change a retention law,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6049)|
| 1:40:53| if we are asking them to do anything that is to determine,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6053)|
| 1:41:01| either directly or indirectly,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6061)|
| 1:41:03| if we are trying to influence legislation, then we are lobbying.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6063)|
| 1:41:09| So there are lots of different ways we communicate.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6069)|
| 1:41:11| Sometimes we educate just sharing information.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6071)|
| 1:41:14| Sometimes we advocate by supporting a position.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6074)|
| 1:41:17| We might support a position with each other here.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6077)|
| 1:41:20| None of that would be lobbying.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6080)|
| 1:41:22| So lobbying is only when we are influencing legislation.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6082)|
| 1:41:26| So it is important that we use that term when that is what we are actually doing.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6086)|
| 1:41:32| Last year, Channel 5 in Nashville did a little study,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6092)|
| 1:41:35| and what they found is that there are 61 lobbyists right now| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6095)|
| 1:41:39| who are working specifically to privatize public schools.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6099)|
| 1:41:43| They are working specifically against us, basically.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6103)|
| 1:41:46| There are 17 public ed lobbyists,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6106)|
| 1:41:49| and of course it is in the interest of the people with the top number| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6109)|
| 1:41:53| to keep the bottom number low.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6113)|
| 1:41:56| There are organizations spending millions of dollars| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6116)|
| 1:41:58| to keep that bottom number low.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6118)|
| 1:42:00| The fewer lobbyists we have working for public education,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6120)|
| 1:42:03| the easier it is for profiteering organizations| [source video](https://archive.org/details/school-board-ws-4178-230905?start=6123)|
